## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / concentration-time ODEs)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time derivative of a concentration A, which is the standard setting of chemical kinetics where rate laws define dA/dt as a function of species concentrations (here only A) and possibly explicit time dependence (e.g., changing conditions or feeds). With only t and A available, the most likely structures are single-species decay/growth, reversible relaxation to equilibrium, autocatalysis, or time-dependent effective rate constants k(t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant production or depletion when reactant is in excess)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (unimolecular decay if c0 < 0, growth if c0 > 0)
- Second-order kinetics (self-reaction): dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular A + A or mean-field quadratic loss)
- Nth-order power-law rate: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general empirical reaction order)
- Linear relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (approach to steady-state concentration c1)
- Affine-in-A rate law: dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A (constant source/sink plus first-order loss/gain)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-type kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-amplification with saturation due to limitation)
- Reversible first-order to equilibrium (scaled form): dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) - c2 * A (net of forward formation toward c1 and backward consumption)
- Rational (inhibition/limitation) rate: dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1) (effective first-order at low A with saturation at high A)
- Rational with decay at high A (substrate inhibition-like): dA_dt = c0 * A / (A**2 + c1) (rate decreases after a peak as A grows)
- Time-dependent first-order rate constant: dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * A (slow drift in conditions leading to changing effective k(t))
- Exponential time-varying rate: dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) * A (activation/deactivation of kinetics over time, e.g., catalyst deactivation/activation proxy)
- Periodic forcing of kinetics: dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (externally modulated environment or feed cycles impacting the effective rate)
- Piecewise-like smooth switch in regime: dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * tanh(c2 * (t - c3))) * A (transition between two kinetic regimes over time)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Reaction order identification: if dA_dt scales approximately proportional to A**n, a power-law term c0 * A**c1 is plausible, with sign indicating production vs consumption.
- Equilibrium approach: if trajectories asymptote to a nonzero constant A*, use linear relaxation c0 * (c1 - A) (or affine-in-A) to represent a stable fixed point.
- Autocatalysis vs limitation: S-shaped time courses often correspond to dA_dt containing A multiplied by a limiting factor (c1 - A), i.e., c0 * A * (c1 - A).
- Inhibition/limitation by high concentration: if rates increase with A then level off or decrease at high A, prefer rational forms like A/(A+c1) (saturation) or A/(A**2+c1) (peaked then decreasing).
- Time-varying environment: if apparent kinetic parameters change over t even at the same A, represent k(t) multiplicatively on A (e.g., (c0 + c1 * t) * A or (c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) * A).
- Externally driven oscillations: periodic patterns in residuals vs t suggest adding sin(c * t) or cos(c * t) to k(t) rather than adding oscillations directly to A-only terms.
- Multiple regimes (switching kinetics): if early-time and late-time behaviors have different effective slopes, a smooth switch factor like tanh(c*(t-c0)) multiplying A can capture regime change without hard discontinuities.
- Physical nonnegativity constraint: for concentrations, rate laws that can drive A negative at small A (e.g., large negative constant c0) are suspect unless modeling a constant sink; prefer A-multiplicative depletion for irreversible decay.

Best expression     : A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4) + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)/sqrt(A)
Structure desc      : top-level additive combination, contains transcendental functions sin, contains fractions, 3 additive terms, complex structure (depth 5)
Fitted params       : c0=-4.6607e-03, c1=-1.0310e-02, c2=-5.0160e-01, c3=8.4804e-01, c4=3.1580e+00, c5=2.0807e-01, c6=5.5342e-01, c7=3.1500e+00
Train NMSE          : 8.16e-14
Test NMSE           : 7.84e-14

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK23)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidate formulas: 53

GT is the fixed function (of \(A\) only)
\[
f(A)= -0.10016955960092372\,\sqrt{A}\;+\;0.47148501687516587\,\sin(0.8555148185506902\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must be expressible as “(constant)\(\cdot\sqrt A\) + (constant)\(\cdot\sin(\text{linear in }A)\)” with **no** extra terms (no constants, no \(A\), no \(A^2\), no logs/exp/rationals, no \(\sin\) with phase shift unless removable, etc.). Also GT has **no** \(t\)-dependence.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether all non-GT-structure terms can be eliminated by setting candidate constants, and whether the remaining structure can exactly match \(-k\sqrt A + m\sin(\omega A)\).

---

### 1.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)+ c5\sin(Ac6+c7)/\sqrt A\).  
Can zero out \(A^2\) and \(A\) terms (set \(c0=c1=0\)) and the \(1/\sqrt A\) term (set \(c5=0\)). Left with \(c2\sin(Ac3+c4)\). Missing the \(-0.1001\sqrt A\) term. **No match**.

### 2.
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A^{c2}c3\sin(Ac4+c5)+c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\).  
Can kill \(A^2,A\) and one sine, but remaining terms are sines times powers of \(A\) or extra sine. No way to produce a standalone \(\sqrt A\) term. **No match**.

### 3.
Rational terms in \(A\), constant, sine, plus log. Even if log and rationals are zeroed, you can at best get constant + sine. No \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 4.
\(A^2\), \(A\), constant, sine, log. Can zero \(A^2,A,\) constant, log leaving sine only. No \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 5.
constant + sine + exp + log. Can zero exp/log/constant leaving sine only. No \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 6.
\(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3 + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)+ c7 e^{Ac8}\).  
Could set \(c0=c3=c7=0\). To get \(\sqrt A\) you might try \(A^{c1}c2\) with \(c1=\tfrac12\), giving \(c2\sqrt A\). Good. But then you still have a sine term \(c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\) which can match the GT sine only if phase shift \(c6=0\). That’s possible. So remaining form can be \(c2\sqrt A + c4\sin(Ac5)\). This can match GT by choosing \(c2=-0.1001695\), \(c4=0.4714850\), \(c5=0.8555148\). **Yes, this candidate can match**—wait: there is also the \(A c0\) term already set to 0, fine. So **Candidate 6 matches**.

(We still continue checking others, but one match is enough for final verdict.)

### 7.
Has \(t/(A c5+c6)\) term; to remove \(t\)-dependence set \(c4=0\). Then has \(1/(A c5+c6)\) and log and constant and sine. Can set those to 0 except sine, but no \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 8.
Has \(A^{c0}c1/(A^{c0}+c2)\) (non-\(\sqrt A\) rational in \(A^{c0}\)), plus sine and log and constant. No way to become exactly \(\sqrt A\) for all \(A\). **No match**.

### 9.
\(A c0 + \frac{A^{c1}c2}{A^{c1}+c3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)+ c7/(Ac8+c9)\).  
Rational terms cannot become \(\sqrt A\) globally; can zero them, but then left with \(A\) and sine. No \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 10.
Similar to 9 but with \(\sin(c5|A|+c6)\) and constant. Still no \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 11.
\(A c0 + c1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)+ c5\log(Ac6+1)+ c7 e^{Ac8}\).  
Can zero everything but sine; no \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 12.
constant + sine + logs. No \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 13.
\(\sqrt A\,c0 + c1\sin(Ac2+c3)\).  
This is exactly the GT structure. Set \(c0=-0.1001695596\), \(c1=0.4714850169\), \(c2=0.8555148186\), \(c3=0\). **Match**.

### 14.
\(\sqrt A\,c0 + c1\sin(c2 + c3|A|)\).  
For \(A\ge 0\), \(|A|=A\), so it can match GT on nonnegative \(A\) by setting \(c2=0\), \(c3=0.8555\). But equivalence is required “for all values of the feature variables”; if \(A\) can be negative, GT has \(\sqrt A\) (not real) while candidate uses \(\sqrt A\) too, so domain issues arise. In typical real-valued setting, both imply \(A\ge 0\). On \(A\ge 0\), it matches. Still, since we already have clear matches (6,13), we don’t need to rely on domain subtleties. **Potential match on \(A\ge0\)**.

### 15.
Complicated rational with \((\sqrt A + c1)\) denominators and extra terms. To remove denominator dependence you’d need impossible cancellations for all \(A\) unless numerator also has same factor; but structure doesn’t reduce cleanly to \(-k\sqrt A + m\sin(\omega A)\) without leftover rational dependence. **No match**.

### 16.
\(A c0 + \frac{A^{c1}c2}{A^{c1}+c3} + c4 + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)+ c8 e^{Ac9}\).  
No \(\sqrt A\) term unless rational becomes \(\sqrt A\) (not possible globally). **No match**.

### 17.
\(\sqrt A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A c3\tanh(c4+c5 t)+ c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\).  
Must remove all \(t\)-dependence: set \(c3=0\). Remove \(A\) terms: set \(c1=c2=0\). Then \(\sqrt A c0 + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\) matches GT with \(c8=0\) and appropriate constants. **Match**.

### 18.
\(\sqrt A c0 + c1\sin(Ac2+c3)+c4\).  
Set \(c4=0\), \(c3=0\), and match coefficients/frequency. **Match**.

### 19.
\(\sqrt A c0 + c1\sin(c2|A|+c3)+c4\).  
On \(A\ge0\), can set \(c4=0,c3=0\) and match. Same domain caveat as 14. **Potential match**.

### 20.
\(A c0/|\sqrt A| + c1\sin(c2|A|+c3)+c4\).  
For \(A>0\), \(A/|\sqrt A|=\sqrt A\). So on positive \(A\), first term is \(\sqrt A c0\). Set \(c4=0,c3=0\) and match. Again domain caveat at \(A=0\) and negative \(A\). But we already have unconditional matches. **Potential match (for \(A>0\))**.

Contains \(A c0\) and a nontrivial exp(cos(log)) term plus sine and constant. Can zero exotic term and \(A c0\), leaving sine + constant; no \(\sqrt A\). **No match**.

### 24.

### 26.
Has \(t\)-dependent tanh term; set its coefficient \(c2=0\). Then has \(A c0 + A c1 + A^{c5}c6 +\) sine. Need \(\sqrt A\): set \(c5=1/2\), \(c6=-0.1001695\), set \(c0=c1=0\), set sine phase 0 and match. **Match**.
